**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Elasticsearch Index Lifecycle Management Policy Engine

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in elastic/elasticsearch under x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/ and server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/metadata/ that implement Index Lifecycle Management (ILM). Identify: the IndexLifecycleService that triggers policy evaluation, the LifecyclePolicy and Phase model classes, the TransportPutLifecycleAction and TransportDeleteLifecycleAction handlers, the step execution framework (ClusterStateActionStep, AsyncWaitStep, AsyncActionStep), and the LifecycleExecutionState stored in index metadata. Report each file path and key class.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the platform domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/elasticsearch--v8.17.0.

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive analysis of the Elasticsearch Index Lifecycle Management (ILM) system and documented all findings in `/workspace/answer.json`.

## Summary

I've identified and documented **27 key Java source files** and **13 major class symbols** that implement the ILM policy engine in Elasticsearch 8.17.0:

### Key Findings:

**Core Components:**
- **Policy Model**: `LifecyclePolicy` and `Phase` define policies and execution phases
- **Step Framework**: Abstract base `Step` class with four execution types:
  - `ClusterStateActionStep` - Synchronous cluster state modifications
  - `ClusterStateWaitStep` - Fast cluster state condition checks
  - `AsyncWaitStep` - Periodic async condition evaluation
  - `AsyncActionStep` - Asynchronous actions (rollover, shrink, etc.)

**Execution Engine:**
- `IndexLifecycleService` - Triggers policy evaluation on schedule and cluster changes
- `IndexLifecycleRunner` - Dispatches steps to appropriate execution handlers
- `PolicyStepsRegistry` - Central registry mapping policies to compiled step sequences

**State Management:**
- `LifecycleExecutionState` - Immutable record storing execution progress in index metadata
- `IndexLifecycleTransition` - Validates and coordinates step transitions
- `PhaseCacheManagement` - Protects from concurrent policy updates

**Transport Handlers:**
- `TransportPutLifecycleAction` - Adds/updates policies
- `TransportDeleteLifecycleAction` - Removes policies
- Plus action handlers for explain, move, retry, status operations

**Cluster State Tasks:**
- `ExecuteStepsUpdateTask` - Executes cluster state action steps
- `MoveToNextStepUpdateTask` - Transitions after async completion

The complete analysis with all file paths, class definitions, and architectural explanation has been written

\"server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/metadata/LifecycleExecutionState.java\",\n      \"symbol\": \"LifecycleExecutionState\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"# Elasticsearch Index Lifecycle Management (ILM) Architecture Analysis\\n\\n## Overview\\nThe Elasticsearch 8.17.0 ILM system is a comprehensive policy-driven index management framework. The implementation spans across three main components: core policy definitions, ILM coordination service, and cluster state management.\\n\\n## Core Components\\n\\n### 1. Policy Model Classes (x-pack/plugin/core/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/core/ilm/)\\n\\n**LifecyclePolicy** (LifecyclePolicy.java)\\n- Represents the lifecycle of an index from creation to deletion\\n- Contains a mapping of phase names to Phase objects\\n- Implements SimpleDiffable<LifecyclePolicy> and ToXContentObject for serialization\\n- Supports TimeseriesLifecycleType and validates phases through LifecycleType\\n- Includes optional metadata and deprecation flags\\n\\n**Phase** (Phase.java)\\n- Represents a set of LifecycleActions to execute at a particular point in index lifecycle\\n- Contains minimum age (TimeValue) and a map of named LifecycleActions\\n- Implements ToXContentObject and Writeable for serialization\\n- Ordered by LifecycleType; actions execute in defined order\\n\\n**Step** (Step.java)\\n- Abstract base class for all ILM execution steps\\n- Contains StepKey (phase, action, name) and next step reference\\n- Subclassed into four main step types:\\n  - ClusterStateActionStep: Updates cluster state, immediate execution\\n  - ClusterStateWaitStep: Waits for cluster state condition\\n  - AsyncActionStep: Performs asynchronous actions via client\\n  - AsyncWaitStep: Periodically checks asynchronous conditions\\n\\n### 2. Step Execution Framework\\n\\n**ClusterStateActionStep** (ClusterStateActionStep.java)\\n- Abstract class for steps that modify cluster state directly\\n- Method: performAction(Index, ClusterState) -> ClusterState\\n- Optional indexForAsyncInvocation() for spawning new indices\\n- Executed synchronously during cluster state update tasks\\n\\n**ClusterStateWaitStep** (ClusterStateWaitStep.java)\\n- Abstract class for steps that wait on cluster state conditions\\n- Method: isConditionMet(IndexMetadata, ClusterState) -> boolean\\n- Fast-path for checks not requiring async operations\\n- Included in periodic policy execution\\n\\n**AsyncWaitStep** (AsyncWaitStep.java)\\n- Abstract class for periodically-evaluated async conditions\\n- Method: evaluateCondition(Metadata, Index, Listener, TimeValue)\\n- Listener callbacks: onResponse(boolean, ToXContentObject) and onFailure(Exception)\\n- Used for checks that may require I/O (e.g., segment count, rollover readiness)\\n\\n**AsyncActionStep** (AsyncActionStep.java)\\n- Abstract class for async actions via transport/client calls\\n- Method: performAction(IndexMetadata, ClusterState, ClusterStateObserver, ActionListener<Void>)\\n- indexSurvives() indicates if action deletes the index\\n- Used for operations like rollover, shrink, force-merge, delete\\n\\n### 3. ILM Service (Policy Evaluator)\\n\\n**IndexLifecycleService** (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/IndexLifecycleService.java)\\n- Implements ClusterStateListener, ClusterStateApplier, SchedulerEngine.Listener\\n- Triggers policy evaluation: scheduled via SchedulerEngine and on cluster changes\\n- Key method: clusterChanged(ClusterChangedEvent) - filters indices and dispatches to IndexLifecycleRunner\\n- Maintains master-only scheduler for policy evaluation\\n- Handles cluster state lifecycle events and index creation\\n- Integrates with PluginShutdownService for graceful shutdown\\n\\n### 4. Policy Execution Engine\\n\\n**IndexLifecycleRunner** (IndexLifecycleRunner.java)\\n- Executes individual step operations from PolicyStepsRegistry\\n- Dispatches step execution to appropriate method based on step type:\\n  - ClusterStateActionStep: submitUnbatchedTask(ExecuteStepsUpdateTask)\\n  - AsyncWaitStep: evaluateCondition() with periodic re-evaluation\\n  - AsyncActionStep: performAction() with client\\n  - ClusterStateWaitStep: immediate condition check\\n- Handles step failure, retry logic, and error step transitions\\n- Updates LifecycleExecutionState in index metadata\\n\\n**PolicyStepsRegistry** (PolicyStepsRegistry.java)\\n- Central registry mapping policy names to compiled step sequences\\n- Maintains: lifecycle policy map, first step cache, step lookups\\n- Updates dynamically as policies change via update(Metadata)\\n- Parses phase definitions from IndexLifecycleMetadata\\n- Provides: getStep(IndexMetadata, StepKey), getIndexAgeForPhase(policy, phase)\\n\\n### 5. Cluster State Update Tasks\\n\\n**ExecuteStepsUpdateTask** (ExecuteStepsUpdateTask.java)\\n- Extends IndexLifecycleClusterStateUpdateTask\\n- Executes ClusterStateActionStep operations\\n- Updates metadata with new step keys and execution state\\n- Deduplicates identical transitions\\n\\n**MoveToNextStepUpdateTask** (MoveToNextStepUpdateTask.java)\\n- Transitions index to next step after async action completes\\n- Updates LifecycleExecutionState with new StepKey\\n- Validates transition legality via IndexLifecycleTransition\\n\\n**IndexLifecycleTransition** (IndexLifecycleTransition.java)\\n- Validates step transitions and policy phase changes\\n- moveClusterStateToNextStep(IndexMetadata, StepKey) -> ClusterState\\n- Manages phase caching via PhaseCacheManagement\\n- Handles policy metadata versioning\\n\\n### 6. Execution State Storage\\n\\n**LifecycleExecutionState** (server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/metadata/LifecycleExecutionState.java)\\n- Record-based immutable state containing:\\n  - Current: phase, action, step\\n  - Error tracking: failedStep, isAutoRetryableError, failedStepRetryCount\\n  - Metadata: stepInfo, previousStepInfo, phaseDefinition\\n  - Timestamps: lifecycleDate, phaseTime, actionTime, stepTime\\n  - Context-specific: snapshotRepository, snapshotName, shrinkIndexName, downsampleIndexName\\n- Serialized as custom metadata in IndexMetadata via ILM_CUSTOM_METADATA_KEY (\\\"ilm\\\")\\n- Builder pattern for construction and modification\\n\\n**IndexMetadata** (server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/metadata/IndexMetadata.java)\\n- Contains LifecycleExecutionState via getLifecycleExecutionState()\\n- Stores lifecycle policy name and execution state\\n\\n### 7. Transport Actions (Policy Management)\\n\\n**TransportPutLifecycleAction** (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/action/TransportPutLifecycleAction.java)\\n- Extends TransportMasterNodeAction<PutLifecycleRequest, AcknowledgedResponse>\\n- Handler: UpdateLifecyclePolicyTask (AckedClusterStateUpdateTask)\\n- Validates policy format via NamedXContentRegistry\\n- Updates IndexLifecycleMetadata in cluster state\\n- Handles policy version management and index metadata updates\\n- Supports SearchableSnapshotAction and WaitForSnapshotAction validation\\n\\n**TransportDeleteLifecycleAction** (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/action/TransportDeleteLifecycleAction.java)\\n- Extends TransportMasterNodeAction<Request, AcknowledgedResponse>\\n- Handler: DeleteLifecyclePolicyTask (AckedClusterStateUpdateTask)\\n- Removes policy from IndexLifecycleMetadata\\n- Ensures no indices reference deleted policy\\n\\n### 8. Additional ILM Actions\\n\\n- TransportGetLifecycleAction: Retrieves stored policies\\n- TransportExplainLifecycleAction: Explains current execution state of indices\\n- TransportMoveToStepAction: Manual step transitions\\n- TransportRetryAction: Retries failed steps\\n\\n### 9. Metadata Management\\n\\n**IndexLifecycleMetadata** (IndexLifecycleMetadata.java)\\n- Cluster-wide container for all ILM policies\\n- Map<String, LifecyclePolicyMetadata> storing policy metadata\\n- OperationMode tracking (RUNNING, STOPPED, STOPPING)\\n\\n**LifecyclePolicyMetadata** (LifecyclePolicyMetadata.java)\\n- Wrapper around LifecyclePolicy with versioning\\n- Stores: policy name, version, creation time, last modified time\\n- Used for policy update detection and consistency\\n\\n**PhaseCacheManagement** (PhaseCacheManagement.java)\\n- Manages cached phase definitions in index metadata\\n- Prevents execution interruption when policies are updated\\n- Methods: refreshPhaseDefinition(), updateIndicesForPolicy()\\n\\n## Execution Flow\\n\\n1. **Policy Trigger**: IndexLifecycleService.clusterChanged() fires on cluster events or scheduled interval\\n2. **Index Discovery**: Service filters indices with active ILM policies\\n3. **Registry Lookup**: PolicyStepsRegistry provides current step for index\\n4. **Step Execution**:\\n   - ClusterStateActionStep: Immediate cluster state update via ExecuteStepsUpdateTask\\n   - AsyncActionStep: Client action dispatch via IndexLifecycleRunner\\n   - AsyncWaitStep: Async condition evaluation with periodic re-check\\n   - ClusterStateWaitStep: Immediate condition evaluation\\n5. **State Transition**: Successful step completion triggers MoveToNextStepUpdateTask\\n6. **Error Handling**: Failures transition to ErrorStep and await manual retry\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Immutable State**: LifecycleExecutionState is a record for thread-safe mutations\\n- **Registry Pattern**: PolicyStepsRegistry centralizes step lookup and caching\\n- **Composite Steps**: Steps compose into phases and policies\\n- **Listener Pattern**: AsyncWaitStep and AsyncActionStep use callbacks for completion\\n- **Cluster Task Deduplication**: IndexLifecycleRunner deduplicates identical transitions\\n- **Phase Caching**: PhaseCacheManagement isolates indices from concurrent policy updates\\n\"\n}\n",

Management (ILM) Architecture Analysis\\n\\n## Overview\\nThe Elasticsearch 8.17.0 ILM system is a comprehensive policy-driven index management framework. The implementation spans across three main components: core policy definitions, ILM coordination service, and cluster state management.\\n\\n## Core Components\\n\\n### 1. Policy Model Classes (x-pack/plugin/core/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/core/ilm/)\\n\\n**LifecyclePolicy** (LifecyclePolicy.java)\\n- Represents the lifecycle of an index from creation to deletion\\n- Contains a mapping of phase names to Phase objects\\n- Implements SimpleDiffable<LifecyclePolicy> and ToXContentObject for serialization\\n- Supports TimeseriesLifecycleType and validates phases through LifecycleType\\n- Includes optional metadata and deprecation flags\\n\\n**Phase** (Phase.java)\\n- Represents a set of LifecycleActions to execute at a particular point in index lifecycle\\n- Contains minimum age (TimeValue) and a map of named LifecycleActions\\n- Implements ToXContentObject and Writeable for serialization\\n- Ordered by LifecycleType; actions execute in defined order\\n\\n**Step** (Step.java)\\n- Abstract base class for all ILM execution steps\\n- Contains StepKey (phase, action, name) and next step reference\\n- Subclassed into four main step types:\\n  - ClusterStateActionStep: Updates cluster state, immediate execution\\n  - ClusterStateWaitStep: Waits for cluster state condition\\n  - AsyncActionStep: Performs asynchronous actions via client\\n  - AsyncWaitStep: Periodically checks asynchronous conditions\\n\\n### 2. Step Execution Framework\\n\\n**ClusterStateActionStep** (ClusterStateActionStep.java)\\n- Abstract class for steps that modify cluster state directly\\n- Method: performAction(Index, ClusterState) -> ClusterState\\n- Optional indexForAsyncInvocation() for spawning new indices\\n- Executed synchronously during cluster state update tasks\\n\\n**ClusterStateWaitStep** (ClusterStateWaitStep.java)\\n- Abstract class for steps that wait on cluster state conditions\\n- Method: isConditionMet(IndexMetadata, ClusterState) -> boolean\\n- Fast-path for checks not requiring async operations\\n- Included in periodic policy execution\\n\\n**AsyncWaitStep** (AsyncWaitStep.java)\\n- Abstract class for periodically-evaluated async conditions\\n- Method: evaluateCondition(Metadata, Index, Listener, TimeValue)\\n- Listener callbacks: onResponse(boolean, ToXContentObject) and onFailure(Exception)\\n- Used for checks that may require I/O (e.g., segment count, rollover readiness)\\n\\n**AsyncActionStep** (AsyncActionStep.java)\\n- Abstract class for async actions via transport/client calls\\n- Method: performAction(IndexMetadata, ClusterState, ClusterStateObserver, ActionListener<Void>)\\n- indexSurvives() indicates if action deletes the index\\n- Used for operations like rollover, shrink, force-merge, delete\\n\\n### 3. ILM Service (Policy Evaluator)\\n\\n**IndexLifecycleService** (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/IndexLifecycleService.java)\\n- Implements ClusterStateListener, ClusterStateApplier, SchedulerEngine.Listener\\n- Triggers policy evaluation: scheduled via SchedulerEngine and on cluster changes\\n- Key method: clusterChanged(ClusterChangedEvent) - filters indices and dispatches to IndexLifecycleRunner\\n- Maintains master-only scheduler for policy evaluation\\n- Handles cluster state lifecycle events and index creation\\n- Integrates with PluginShutdownService for graceful shutdown\\n\\n### 4. Policy Execution Engine\\n\\n**IndexLifecycleRunner** (IndexLifecycleRunner.java)\\n- Executes individual step operations from PolicyStepsRegistry\\n- Dispatches step execution to appropriate method based on step type:\\n  - ClusterStateActionStep: submitUnbatchedTask(ExecuteStepsUpdateTask)\\n  - AsyncWaitStep: evaluateCondition() with periodic re-evaluation\\n  - AsyncActionStep: performAction() with client\\n  - ClusterStateWaitStep: immediate condition check\\n- Handles step failure, retry logic, and error step transitions\\n- Updates LifecycleExecutionState in index metadata\\n\\n**PolicyStepsRegistry** (PolicyStepsRegistry.java)\\n- Central registry mapping policy names to compiled step sequences\\n- Maintains: lifecycle policy map, first step cache, step lookups\\n- Updates dynamically as policies change via update(Metadata)\\n- Parses phase definitions from IndexLifecycleMetadata\\n- Provides: getStep(IndexMetadata, StepKey), getIndexAgeForPhase(policy, phase)\\n\\n### 5. Cluster State Update Tasks\\n\\n**ExecuteStepsUpdateTask** (ExecuteStepsUpdateTask.java)\\n- Extends IndexLifecycleClusterStateUpdateTask\\n- Executes ClusterStateActionStep operations\\n- Updates metadata with new step keys and execution state\\n- Deduplicates identical transitions\\n\\n**MoveToNextStepUpdateTask** (MoveToNextStepUpdateTask.java)\\n- Transitions index to next step after async action completes\\n- Updates LifecycleExecutionState with new StepKey\\n- Validates transition legality via IndexLifecycleTransition\\n\\n**IndexLifecycleTransition** (IndexLifecycleTransition.java)\\n- Validates step transitions and policy phase changes\\n- moveClusterStateToNextStep(IndexMetadata, StepKey) -> ClusterState\\n- Manages phase caching via PhaseCacheManagement\\n- Handles policy metadata versioning\\n\\n### 6. Execution State Storage\\n\\n**LifecycleExecutionState** (server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/metadata/LifecycleExecutionState.java)\\n- Record-based immutable state containing:\\n  - Current: phase, action, step\\n  - Error tracking: failedStep, isAutoRetryableError, failedStepRetryCount\\n  - Metadata: stepInfo, previousStepInfo, phaseDefinition\\n  - Timestamps: lifecycleDate, phaseTime, actionTime, stepTime\\n  - Context-specific: snapshotRepository, snapshotName, shrinkIndexName, downsampleIndexName\\n- Serialized as custom metadata in IndexMetadata via ILM_CUSTOM_METADATA_KEY (\\\"ilm\\\")\\n- Builder pattern for construction and modification\\n\\n**IndexMetadata** (server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/metadata/IndexMetadata.java)\\n- Contains LifecycleExecutionState via getLifecycleExecutionState()\\n- Stores lifecycle policy name and execution state\\n\\n### 7. Transport Actions (Policy Management)\\n\\n**TransportPutLifecycleAction** (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/action/TransportPutLifecycleAction.java)\\n- Extends TransportMasterNodeAction<PutLifecycleRequest, AcknowledgedResponse>\\n- Handler: UpdateLifecyclePolicyTask (AckedClusterStateUpdateTask)\\n- Validates policy format via NamedXContentRegistry\\n- Updates IndexLifecycleMetadata in cluster state\\n- Handles policy version management and index metadata updates\\n- Supports SearchableSnapshotAction and WaitForSnapshotAction validation\\n\\n**TransportDeleteLifecycleAction** (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/action/TransportDeleteLifecycleAction.java)\\n- Extends TransportMasterNodeAction<Request, AcknowledgedResponse>\\n- Handler: DeleteLifecyclePolicyTask (AckedClusterStateUpdateTask)\\n- Removes policy from IndexLifecycleMetadata\\n- Ensures no indices reference deleted policy\\n\\n### 8. Additional ILM Actions\\n\\n- TransportGetLifecycleAction: Retrieves stored policies\\n- TransportExplainLifecycleAction: Explains current execution state of indices\\n- TransportMoveToStepAction: Manual step transitions\\n- TransportRetryAction: Retries failed steps\\n\\n### 9. Metadata Management\\n\\n**IndexLifecycleMetadata** (IndexLifecycleMetadata.java)\\n- Cluster-wide container for all ILM policies\\n- Map<String, LifecyclePolicyMetadata> storing policy metadata\\n- OperationMode tracking (RUNNING, STOPPED, STOPPING)\\n\\n**LifecyclePolicyMetadata** (LifecyclePolicyMetadata.java)\\n- Wrapper around LifecyclePolicy with versioning\\n- Stores: policy name, version, creation time, last modified time\\n- Used for policy update detection and consistency\\n\\n**PhaseCacheManagement** (PhaseCacheManagement.java)\\n- Manages cached phase definitions in index metadata\\n- Prevents execution interruption when policies are updated\\n- Methods: refreshPhaseDefinition(), updateIndicesForPolicy()\\n\\n## Execution Flow\\n\\n1. **Policy Trigger**: IndexLifecycleService.clusterChanged() fires on cluster events or scheduled interval\\n2. **Index Discovery**: Service filters indices with active ILM policies\\n3. **Registry Lookup**: PolicyStepsRegistry provides current step for index\\n4. **Step Execution**:\\n   - ClusterStateActionStep: Immediate cluster state update via ExecuteStepsUpdateTask\\n   - AsyncActionStep: Client action dispatch via IndexLifecycleRunner\\n   - AsyncWaitStep: Async condition evaluation with periodic re-check\\n   - ClusterStateWaitStep: Immediate condition evaluation\\n5. **State Transition**: Successful step completion triggers MoveToNextStepUpdateTask\\n6. **Error Handling**: Failures transition to ErrorStep and await manual retry\\n\\n## Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Immutable State**: LifecycleExecutionState is a record for thread-safe mutations\\n- **Registry Pattern**: PolicyStepsRegistry centralizes step lookup and caching\\n- **Composite Steps**: Steps compose into phases and policies\\n- **Listener Pattern**: AsyncWaitStep and AsyncActionStep use callbacks for completion\\n- **Cluster Task Deduplication**: IndexLifecycleRunner deduplicates identical transitions\\n- **Phase Caching**: PhaseCacheManagement isolates indices from concurrent policy updates\\n\"\n}\n",
